Pope attacked the Treasury Department for its ineffective silver purchases and said that he was willing to support a return to a silver standard for the US dollar at a ratio of sixteen to one for gold and silver. Pope also admitted that he was drafting a proposal to make the gold-silver ratio vary according to the amount of silver produced in the world. Although the average gold-silver ratio has been sixteen to one for the past ten years, there should be room for adjustment if the production volume in the future is very different. Pope believed that after the price of silver rises, the United States may not have to worry about excessive imports of foreign silver, because foreign countries have recently been unwilling to sell, which is sufficient to show that there is not much silver in storage, and production has not increased. Therefore, a higher price can slightly stimulate the increase in production, and the whole world can benefit from its stimulation and develop a healthy economic situation. (National News Agency, 10th)

Roosevelt Advocates Stable International Currency

Japan Willing to Participate in International Conference

(Washington) It was learned from authoritative sources this morning that President Roosevelt is eager for international cooperation to seek currency stability. This international cooperation can be obtained at the International Monetary Conference, and this International Monetary Conference may resolve the world's currency war. It is learned that the price of the US dollar will remain at 59.06 before the International Conference is held. (National News Agency, 10th)

(Tokyo) According to foreign wire reports, US President Roosevelt will convene a world economic conference to seek the agreement of various countries on measures such as reducing tariffs, abolishing import restrictions, and prohibiting imports in order to promote world trade. However, according to later reports, it is quite doubtful whether the US President actually has this intention. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs expressed its opinion on this issue, saying that if this news is true, the Japanese government is happy to participate in the conference and strive to reform the world's economic state. The world economic conference should first carefully study all the reasons that hinder trade, prohibit raising tariffs, allocate import quotas, prohibit imports, and all other policies that hinder trade. Finally, it is necessary to agree on exchange rates in order to smooth trade. (Japan United Press, 11th)

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Finance announced that the amount of gold purchased up to December 29 last year was 20,951 kilograms, and the purchase price reached 84.789 million yuan. Also, the amount of gold purchase certificates that the government delivered to the Bank of Japan due to the purchase of gold reached 43.521 million yuan. The difference between the government's remaining gold purchase amount and the limit of 100 million yuan is only 56.479 million yuan. The Ministry of Finance feels that this remaining amount is not enough due to the increase in the purchase price, and it plans to increase it by another 100 million to 200 million yuan and decided to submit an amendment to the law at the next meeting. (Dentsu News Agency, 11th)

(London) The London financial community was shocked to hear that the Japanese government increased the price of gold, but according to general opinion, this move is entirely influenced by domestic factors and has nothing to do with restoring the gold standard. (National News Agency, 10th)

Dutch-Japanese Negotiations Fail

Dutch East Indies Intensifies Exclusion of Japanese Goods

Japanese Merchants Panic Upon Hearing the News

(Tokyo) According to the Tokyo News, the Dutch East Indies government is preparing to further restrict the import of Japanese goods. The restricted items are bicycles, paint, and several other items. (China United Press, 11th)

Kobe The Japanese government representatives and their entourage, a total of six people, who participated in the Dutch-Japanese negotiations, returned to Kobe on the Hakozaki Maru on the 10th. Government advisor Shizutaro Kamisaka said that the reason for the failure of the Dutch-Japanese negotiations was that problems such as the cotton cloth import allocation issue, the shipping issue, and the sugar issue arose at every turn, and they could not be resolved. The failure of the Kobe Maritime Conference means that the Batavia negotiations have also naturally disappeared. Therefore, the Kobe conference is the key to future Dutch-Japanese negotiations. If New Naval Treaty Fails, Britain Will Expand Its Navy

And Actively Develop Air Force

(London) According to the Daily Telegraph's naval reporter, Mr. Hayward, if the naval conference fails to establish a new treaty, the British Admiralty admits that there should be a large naval plan for a supplementary fleet in 1936. The naval budget for 1935 stipulates the construction of two or three 9,000-ton cruisers, one light cruiser, eight destroyers, and three submarines. The number of naval officers and soldiers will also increase. In addition, air defense preparations will be actively carried out, the offensive air force will be developed, and aircraft lift equipment will be installed on larger battleships. (National News Agency, 11th)

US Naval Authorities Do Not Favor Pocket Battleships

Still Use Heavy Battleships as Main Force

(Washington) Although pocket battleships have attracted the attention of European political and naval circles, the US naval community does not consider them worthwhile. The Associated Press asked the naval authorities what kind of new battleships the US Navy would build after the naval treaty was abandoned and naval shipbuilding competition became a public fact. Senior naval authorities replied that the United States would continue to build a balanced fleet. In other words, large battleships, aircraft carriers, and armored heavy cruisers will still be the main force of the navy. Destroyers and auxiliary ships will continue to be built to ensure that their numbers are proportional to the number of battleships already built and under construction. Pocket battleships are only welcomed by countries with severely restricted fleets and countries that cannot build heavy battleships due to treaty relations. However, they are ineffective against current and future battleships, because the heavy artillery and weapons of battleships can destroy these pocket battleships. Moreover, pocket battleships have not attracted the attention of Japan and Britain. After the current naval treaty is abolished, the two countries will continue to seek fleet balance in their shipbuilding plans and will increase the number of battleships proportionally. Neither Britain nor Japan is willing to build pocket battleships or indiscriminately build submarines or light cruisers with insufficient power, thereby weakening their national defenses. (National News Agency, 11th)

France Also Controls Industry

Minister of Commerce Submits Bill to the House of Representatives

(Paris) Minister of Commerce Marchandeau has submitted a bill to the House of Representatives to allow France to implement industry regulations that are largely the same as those implemented by the US Reconstruction Agency. These agreements must be initiated by private individuals and exercised by the government. The industries stipulated in the bill are limited to those currently in difficulty. The main points are to limit working hours, preserve inventories, and issue bonds, which are closely related to the national economy. (Reuters, 10th)

Contents of the British-Indian Trade Agreement

(London) The British-Indian trade agreement was signed in London yesterday. This is the result of the Lancashire direct delegation to India in 1933 for negotiations. Its main provisions are that Indian industries can obtain the protection necessary to ensure fair prices for Indian products and imported goods. According to this principle, the import tax on British goods will be lower than that on foreign goods, and this difference must not be changed to the disadvantage of Britain. The government recognizes that import taxes are an indispensable source of revenue for the Indian government and acknowledges that national tax revenues must be given significant consideration when setting import taxes. At the same time, the Indian government promises to apply high tax rates only to goods that require protective taxes in terms of tax concepts. The Indian government also promises that British industries will have full opportunity to present their cases to the Indian Tax Council. In another exchange of letters, the Indian government reiterated that it would reduce the cotton cloth tax when national tax revenues can eliminate the 5% surtax. In return, the British government will provide some guarantees for the treatment of Indian cotton cloth in the colonies and will cooperate with commercial organizations to develop the trade of Indian raw materials or semi-manufactured goods, such as cotton, imported into British colonies. The effective period of this trade agreement is transferred along with the Ottawa Agreement. After the signing of this agreement, India is on an equal footing with overseas autonomous territories in cotton goods and steel goods according to the Ottawa Agreement. (Reuters, 11th)

Persia to be Renamed Iran Starting March 21

Persia's Capital Persia will change its name to the State of Iran starting March 21 (the Persian New Year). Persian Foreign Minister Kazemi recently sent a letter to the diplomatic representatives of various countries stationed in Persia, explaining the reasons for changing the name. He said that this move is widely supported by public opinion, because the name "Persia," in its original meaning, is only a province of the Persian Empire in history and geography. Therefore, it is appropriate to change the name to "Iran." (Havas, 10th)

ILO Report

Advocates Implementation of Public Works Policy

(Geneva) The International Labor Office issued a report advocating the implementation of a public works policy to reduce and prevent unemployment. Each country should establish an agency to implement the policy, and an international central agency should be established to cooperate with each country to achieve the effect of coordination. As for the policy of regulating prices, a laissez-faire approach should be adopted during periods of economic panic, while a restrictive approach should be adopted during prosperous periods. (Havas, 10th)

Japan Adopts Streamlined Trains

(Tokyo) 1935 marks the era of streamlined practicality. The Ministry of Railways is using projectile-shaped streamlined gasoline trains, currently being rushed into production by Kawasaki Shipbuilding Company. Each train costs 36,000 yuan, is 20 meters long, with sharp, elongated front and rear sections resembling projectiles. It is equipped with a 150-horsepower engine, achieving an average speed of 85 kilometers per hour and a maximum speed of 120 kilometers per hour, making it the fastest land transportation in Japan, reaching world-class speed standards. Each train can accommodate 120 passengers and is scheduled to run on the Yokohama-Hachioji, Hiroshima-Kure, Nagoya-Takefuyo, and Ichikawa-Chiba lines starting in April, facilitating transportation for metropolitan passengers. (11th, Rengo dispatch)

Saar General Election Tomorrow, Europe Reveals Signs of Unease

France, Italy, and Austria Deploy Troops on the Border

Large Numbers of Voters Enter the Saar

(London) As the date of the Saar plebiscite approaches, governments across Europe are showing signs of unease. According to reliable sources, the Austrian and Italian governments are on high alert, fearing that unexpected incidents may follow the German victory in the Saar. It is reported that Italian troops are now heavily concentrated on the Austrian border. If the German National Socialist Party attempts to stage an uprising in Austria after the Saar plebiscite, Italian troops will intervene to deal with it. (11th, Reuters dispatch)

(Paris) The French military authorities are carrying out large-scale defense work on the Saar border for the Saar vote on Sunday. Eleven mobile gendarmerie teams and vehicles are distributed at key locations, and 48 tax police teams are serving as reserves. (10th, Guomin dispatch)

Saarbrücken, Saar 665 Dutch and Swiss civil servants serving as chairmen of various polling stations have arrived here by special train and car, without incident en route. (10th, Havas dispatch)

Saarbrücken, Saar Sixty more South American Saarlanders arrived yesterday to participate in the plebiscite. More than 50,000 people are coming from Germany tomorrow specifically for this matter. It is expected that there will be a grand welcome, and maintaining order will be very difficult. Those who arrived yesterday were greeted with various slogans, some shouting "Long live Hitler," some calling for maintaining the status quo, and others singing the Internationale. At that time, the Wauberg Hall will use radio to announce the results to eight European countries, and then journalists will be allowed to transmit the voting process to the outside by telegraph or telephone. The purpose of the authorities using radio to broadcast the voting results is to allow people to listen at home, so as to avoid crowds gathering in the streets. (11th, Reuters dispatch)

Heads of Polling Stations Sworn In

Saarbrücken, Saar A total of 901 election stations have been set up throughout the Saar region for the plebiscite, each with a head. Among them, 300 are Swiss, 350 are Dutch, 230 are from the Grand Duchy of Luxembourg, and the rest belong to the people of various neutral countries. This morning, 901 heads were sworn in at the Waldburg Assembly Hall here. The entire Plebiscite Committee attended to supervise the oath. The chairman of the committee, Swedish citizen Rohde, made a brief speech, followed by dividing into three groups. The Swiss heads swore before Swiss member Henry, the Dutch heads swore before Dutch member de Jong, and the Luxembourg and other national heads swore before Rohde, saying, "I swear to perform the power I have accepted with honor and conscience." There were no witnesses present at the time of the oath. After the ceremony, the heads returned to the assembly hall. The chairman of the committee, Rohde, ordered all reporters and photographers to leave, and then issued instructions. According to general knowledge, the content of these instructions is to take preventive measures to ensure that the vote is kept secret and no fraud occurs, and to request military police intervention if necessary. (11th, Havas dispatch)

German Side Prepares to Celebrate

Saarbrücken, Saar As the date of the Saar regional plebiscite draws nearer, the political mood of the Saar people is becoming increasingly tense. Although no serious clashes have occurred in recent days, minor incidents have occurred frequently. The sharp confrontation between the pro-German and pro-status quo factions can be seen here. Yesterday, several newspaper vendors of a pro-status quo newspaper were beaten by National Socialists on the street, one of whom lost an eye. In the afternoon, a group of Saarlanders residing in the United States arrived here, and the National Socialists took the opportunity to hold a demonstration. If the police had not intervened, a serious fight would have broken out. As the voting date approaches, the National Socialists have doubled their efforts in propaganda. Relying on their large number, they intimidate the small number of pro-status quo supporters who are unwilling to express opposition to the current system. The National Socialists do not hesitate to use terrorist tactics. The pro-German faction is very confident of victory in the voting results. The German Front has posted notices everywhere, preparing to celebrate the return of the Saar region to Germany. The squares are filled with piles of pine branches for decoration, and residents have prepared bamboo poles to hang celebratory flags. Today, another large group of voters will arrive here from Germany by special train. It is generally expected that the National Socialists will take the opportunity to hold a large-scale demonstration. (11th, Havas dispatch)

Pro-French Posters Discovered

Saarbrücken, Saar Yesterday, huge pro-French posters suddenly appeared on major streets, saying that if the residents of the Saar wish to maintain the status quo, France will not stand in the way. If the residents wish to retain the French franc currency and market, France is willing to accept them happily. France guarantees all rights, without distinction of race, language, or opinion. France is a land of freedom and humanity, etc. Those who saw it were shocked. The police then tore it down on the order of their superiors, but soon the plebiscite committee ordered them not to tear it down, because it was rumored that it was posted by the pro-French faction. (11th, Reuters dispatch)

(Paris) The French authorities firmly believe that if the voting results are favorable to Germany, a large number of people will leave the Saar for France. For the safety of these expatriates, the French authorities have made detailed preparations. The whole country can accommodate 40,000 expatriates. It is said that these expatriates who must move into France after the vote are the separatist communists and terrorists. Their actions in the Saar have been deeply dissatisfied with the local people, so it is necessary to relocate them for good. (10th, Guomin dispatch)

France-Italy Rome Agreement What Austria Looks Forward To

Austrian Foreign Minister Issues Declaration

(Vienna) Austrian Foreign Minister Weidg recently issued a declaration to a Havas reporter, saying that the work recently completed in Rome by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval is very important from both a European and Central European perspective. This kind of work is what we have been looking forward to day and night. The Rome Agreement is enough to give the lasting understanding between Italy and Yugoslavia a solid hope, and the same is true for Hungary and Yugoslavia. Once the convention of mutual non-interference in internal affairs is established, the right to asylum for political prisoners can have a limitation agreed upon by all countries, and will not be abused. The result of the Rome Agreement will first be the separate conclusion of bilateral agreements by the countries of Central Europe, and then enter the stage of mutual consultation in the event of an emergency. If so, it is equivalent to the establishment of a new Vienna Conference, and Europe will obtain lasting peace. We do not believe that the Pan-European policy has the possibility of realization at present, but an economic Pan-European alliance can definitely be gradually realized in the future. This must be based on the France-Italy agreement. It is for this reason that the close relationship between France and Italy is worth celebrating. Fujian Province Pacification Conference Opens

Over 60 Proposals Passed

(Xiamen) The Pacification Conference continued at 9:30 on the 11th. The number of attendees was the same as yesterday. It closed at 5:00 pm, passing 67 proposals, including 13 on reorganizing local troops and suppressing remnant bandits, 10 on training the people and clearing villages, 12 on building roads and adding telegraphs and telephones, 15 on pacifying refugees and post-disaster relief, 3 on boosting the economy and assisting rural areas, 2 on promoting the New Life Movement, 4 on the powers and funding of each pacification zone, and 8 on military transportation. Chiang Ting-wen addressed the conference, saying that the people's armed forces in Fujian have a special situation, with a very large number, most of whom have participated in the revolution. He has jointly verified with Chairman Chen and separately compiled them into provincial security regiments and county security teams, actively reorganized and trained them. In case a few do not cherish themselves and eventually become evil, we will actively handle them according to the purpose of pacification. (10th, Special dispatch)

(Fuzhou) The Pacification Conference closed today. Military officers can return to their defenses immediately. The proposals will be submitted to the Pacification Office for implementation separately. Chen Yifeng, Commissioner of the Seventh District, telegraphed on the 10th that he had arrived in Longyan to take office. (11th, Special dispatch)

(Fuzhou) The Zhangzhou Pacification Office issued a general order to each division, stating that due to years of war, both spiritual and material elements are lacking in soundness, and it is urgent to reorganize them to become elite troops. It ordered each division to formulate plans based on the actual situation, regarding the training of officers, the replenishment of soldiers, the improvement of education, and the replenishment of equipment, and to present them at the upcoming Zhangzhou conference for separate discussions. (11th, Central News Agency dispatch)

The remaining roads will be repaired successively in subsequent years, taking into consideration the local harvest conditions. Furthermore, bridges on various roads have traditionally been funded by special construction levies from the counties. To alleviate the hardships of the people, it is proposed to provide subsidies from the income of the Motor Road Bureau. (Central News Agency Telegram, 11th)

International Commercial Telegraph

Reuters Special Business News Telegram, January 11th

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today's gold price rose by five pence, the price being one hundred and forty-one shillings, nine and a half pence.

London Bar Silver: Today's silver price, spot is 24 pence 4375, futures is 24 pence 5625, both down 125. The main reason is the resale by India and speculators, but the United States and China bought in when the price fell, and the close was stable.

Mount Lyell Silver: Today's silver market, futures fell by thirty pounds sterling, due to poor London telegrams.

Exchange Rates

British-American: London foreign exchange market conditions, again deserted this morning, the opening price for the British-American exchange rate was four dollars, ninety-one cents, one-eight-seven-five, lower than yesterday's American-British closing price by one-eight-seven-five. At eleven o'clock, it rose two-five, and at noon it rose one-two-five again, reaching four dollars, ninety-one cents, five-six-two-five. This price did not change at two o'clock in the afternoon. Also, one US dollar is equal to four shillings and zero-eight-two-four British gold.

British-French: The opening price was 74 francs 15, lower than yesterday by thirteen pounds sterling. At eleven o'clock it rose six pounds sterling, and at noon it rose seven pounds sterling again, reaching 74 francs 28. There was not much fluctuation after that.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton: Today's cotton market opened without much change, but in the first hour, the price fell slightly. Sales from Liverpool and the South were absorbed by the demand from the industry.

New York Wheat: Wheat and coarse grains both fell slightly at the opening, but due to strong spot prices, the market stabilized after the price fell.

Liverpool Wheat: Today's wheat market at 1:00 p.m., the May contract price was five shillings, two and one-two-five pence, the same as yesterday's closing price.

Liverpool Cotton: Today's cotton market at 1:00 p.m., the May contract price was 6.89, up two pounds sterling.

Silk Market

New York: The silk market opened, up one and a half points. Of the price increases in today's commodity market, only silk has increased.

Rubber

London: Today's market conditions opened stable, but at noon, the trading price for the April-May contract was six pence 75, lower than yesterday's closing price by one-two-five. This morning's decline was due to the gradual increase in inventories.

New York: Today, due to the loosening of London market prices, the opening fell eleven to twelve pounds sterling. After the fall, there were not many buyers, so the price still has a tendency to fall further.

Securities

New York: Hopeson & Company reported that the factors favoring the market conditions before the opening of securities were: (1) Although the securities market's upward trend continues to be hindered, there is no sign of an increase in bull closings; (2) The improvement in public utility stocks seems to indicate that the bull closing of public utility stocks has now stopped. The factors unfavorable to the market conditions are that the US Supreme Court is currently considering whether the abolition of the gold clause in debt contracts is legal. This matter continues to restrict securities trading. Trading can be expected to develop after this case is decided.

According to Reuters, the most attention on Wall Street this morning was focused on the question of whether the government's abolition of the gold clause on bonds, which is now being fought in the Supreme Court, is legal. Merchants are now eagerly awaiting the concrete results of this case. At the same time, the activity of the securities market is bound to be restricted by this. The securities market opened this morning, and market conditions were deserted, with minimal trading. Various stocks mostly rose slightly, oil stocks seem to be trending downwards again, and railway stocks are also under slight pressure. Industrial stocks are still being bought, and US steel stocks had more trading at the opening. It is said that market conditions may be slightly firmer today, but selective buying will ultimately be hindered by the general upward trend. The New York securities market prices are listed on the left.

New Siberian Railway (Vladivostok Correspondence)

Developing Coal, Iron, and Oil

Establishing Military Transportation

The industrial development order of advanced industrialized nations generally starts with light industry, as was the case with England. Similarly, the industrial advancement of less developed industrial countries also progresses from light industry to heavy industry, as seen in Japan. This is because light industry focuses on the production of daily necessities for the people, making it easier to find markets for these products both domestically and abroad, leading to profitable individual operations. The Soviet Union is an exception. From the beginning of the first five-year plan, it concentrated all its efforts on heavy industry. Now, the European part of the Soviet Union is quite developed. For example, pig iron production is projected to be over 10 million tons in 1934, ranking second in the world, only after the United States, and five times more than Japan. Steel production is estimated to be over 9.3 million tons in 1934, surpassing England, but still lower than the United States and Germany, yet two and a half times that of Japan.

The Soviet Union is not satisfied with this. Developing only the European part of the country is insufficient, especially since its industrial construction goal is to reach the level of the most prosperous United States in 1929, using the U.S. heavy industry as a benchmark. Now that the first five-year plan is largely completed and the second five-year plan has begun, Siberia, especially Eastern Siberia, cannot be ignored. To develop it, the existing Siberian Railway, even with double tracks, is still not enough. Furthermore, the vast plains in the northern region contain extremely rich deposits of coal, iron, oil, gold, and other minerals.

According to recent surveys, the Bureya coal mine has reserves of 500 billion tons, and the iron ore in the southern part of the Lesser Khingan Range has reserves of 420 million tons. Combining these two major mining areas could form a massive metallurgical industrial complex, known as the "Bureya-Loso Troitsky" region. There is also oil north of Lake Baikal, connected to the oil fields in northern Sakhalin Island, and gold mines near Botapo and in the middle reaches of the Zeya River. These are all special products of Eastern Siberia, enough to make it prosperous and open up new areas in the future. However, the Siberian Railway cannot accomplish this task, and even building branch lines from the Ussuri Railway is insufficient.

Therefore, this autumn, planning began to start from "Tayshet," west of Irkutsk, passing through Bratsk, Botapo, the plains north of Lake Tunguska, crossing the Aldan River, and going through Chunta to Nikolayevsk-on-Amur (庙街) at the mouth of the Amur River. Another plan involves following the same route to "Chunta" and then turning southeast, passing through the aforementioned Bureya-Loso Troitsky industrial area, crossing the Amur River, and ending at Sovetskaya Gavan (蘇維特灣). There are three branch lines: one connecting along the Amur River with Khabarovsk (伯力), one passing through the coal and iron area to "Bilakan" (畢拉干), and one from Chunta to Tynda (塔虎德米格搭), the center of the Amur Railway. The total length of this route is over 1,800 kilometers, and the three branch lines are 720 kilometers long, collectively named the BAM (Baikal-Amur Mainline) railway. It bypasses "Baikal" and "Magistralny," taking the first letter of each place name. The most difficult aspect of the route is the sparse population and insufficient supplies. The Soviet government has started transporting tens of thousands of semi-forced laborers to that area, building temporary housing, and encouraging people to live in that area for development. People who go to that area receive considerable preferential treatment.

The industrial significance, as briefly described above, demonstrates its importance, but the actual content is more than that. The Soviet Union's hypothetical international enemy in the Far East is well-known. In case of an emergency, there are only about 200,000 troops stationed from Chita to Vladivostok. Such a long route and such a vast wilderness make it very difficult to transport troops from Europe, requiring a journey of more than ten days. The opponent, however, has much greater convenience. Therefore, they believe that the connection between the Amur Railway and the Ussuri Railway is likely to be attacked, and they cannot guarantee the speed and safety of military transport. However, the Soviet Union is determined to defend its territory and maintain its natural resources. Therefore, the Siberian Railway cannot fully bear this task. Hence, the ABM (sic) railway project is planned to be completed in two more winters. Currently, the aforementioned three branch lines are being constructed first, with the line from Chunta to Tynda being completed first. Work has also started along the Amur River to Khabarovsk. The progress of the project is difficult for outsiders to understand because it is military in nature. In short, the ABM (sic) railway has particularly significant meaning. (December 30th)

Ceremony for Naming and Presenting Five Aircraft Donated by the People of Peiping City

Five Elders Perform Ribbon-Cutting Ceremony

Peiping Correspondence: The Joint Association for National Salvation Donations of Peiping City dedicated five Fleet training aircraft to the government. This afternoon (8th) at 1:00 PM, a naming and presentation ceremony was held at Nanyuan Airfield. The association had made thorough preparations beforehand. Apart from group representatives, many individual citizens participated. On the Nanyuan motor road, cars, rickshaws, and bicycles were continuously arriving as early as 12:00 noon. Some even walked. Order along the way was maintained by the Fourth Security Team, led by Captain Wang Jialu, who set up temporary posts. At the airfield, soldiers from the Second Division of Guan Linzheng's troops and the 716th and 646th Regiments of Shang Zhen's 32nd Army set up posts. At 3:30 PM, amidst cheers from the crowd, the ceremony was declared complete. The various aspects of the event are detailed below:

Attendance: Attendees included over a hundred representatives from the Political Readjustment Committee (政整會) (Zhang Jianchu), the Military Sub-Committee (军分会) (Xu Ying), the City Party Headquarters (Chen Shiquan), the Provincial Party Headquarters (Chen Fangxian), the Chamber of Commerce (Leng Jiaji), the Director of the Health Bureau (Fang Guji), and the President of Chaoyang University (Jiang Yong). Representatives from various schools and organizations numbered about 3,000, and over a thousand citizens participated freely. In total, the number of attendees was over 5,000.

Venue Arrangement: A rostrum was set up in front of the China National Aviation Corporation warehouse at Nanyuan Airfield. To the left of the rostrum was a lounge and a decorated archway with a banner that read, "Donating Money to Buy Aircraft is an Expression of the People's National Salvation," in powerful calligraphy. The entrance to the venue had a decorated archway with the words "Naming and Presentation Ceremony of Aircraft Donated by the Citizens of Peiping City." The airfield was guarded by various units stationed at Nanyuan, and police officers from the Fourth Security Team and the Southern Suburb Police were stationed in front of the gate.

Appearance of the Five Aircraft: The five aircraft were lined up in front of the rostrum. The fuselages were yellow, and the names of the manufacturers were on the tails. Soldiers from the Fourth Security Team guarded the front and rear of the aircraft. Red silk ribbons were tied to the rear of the aircraft for the five elders to cut during the ribbon-cutting ceremony. The attending crowd eagerly admired the majestic appearance of the five aircraft.

Arrival of the Five Elders: The five elders invited by the donation association to perform the ribbon-cutting ceremony were Jiang Han (79 years old), Xu Fuhai (85 years old), Zhou Shanfu (80 years old), Feng Zhuxuan (82 years old), and Zhang Xiuran (70 years old). They arrived by car at 12:45 PM, escorted by receptionists from the association. They rested in the lounge. The elders were in good spirits, walked strongly, had a kind demeanor, and spoke gently, which inspired reverence from the crowd.

Opening Ceremony: At 12:50 PM, Mayor Yuan Liang arrived. Preparations were immediately made to begin the ceremony. Guests gathered below the rostrum. The chairman of the ceremony, Yuan Liang, Central Government representative Huang Bingheng, members of the City Party Headquarters Chen Shiquan, Xiao Xun, and Xu Xiaoyan, member of the Provincial Party Headquarters Chen Fangxian, representative of the Chamber of Commerce Leng Jiaji, and members of the donation association Wu Chengshi and Yu Shiyuan were all seated on the rostrum. The Public Security Bureau band played music on the side of the rostrum. After performing the rituals, Yuan Liang delivered the opening speech.

Yuan Liang's Speech: He stated that today's naming ceremony of the five aircraft dedicated to the Central Government by Peiping City was honored by the presence of Director Huang Bingheng, dispatched from the Central Government to accept the donation. Mr. Huang is a pioneer in the aviation industry and a first-class figure in Chinese aviation. This proves the importance the Central Government attaches to this matter. He expressed his gratitude to Mr. Huang for his visit and his respect to the Central Government. He also thanked Captain Gao Zhihang of the Air Force for leading his aircraft to participate in the grand ceremony on behalf of all the citizens of the city. Next, Wu Chenghuang, a standing committee member of the donation association, gave a detailed report on the process of purchasing the aircraft. Then, guest speakers gave speeches.

Ribbon-Cutting and Naming: After the speeches, Mayor Yuan Liang led the five elders to the rear of the five aircraft to prepare for the ribbon-cutting ceremony. Amidst the sound of firecrackers and music, the solemn ribbon-cutting ceremony was successfully completed. The five aircraft were piloted by Air Force Captain Gao Zhihang, Deputy Captain Liu Cuigang, and team members Hao Hongzao, Li Kezhi, Dong Mingde, and Yu Tianmin, who boarded the aircraft in preparation for takeoff. At the same time, the names of the five aircraft were announced as "Peiping City No. 1," "Peiping City No. 2," "Peiping City No. 3," "Peiping City No. 4," and "Peiping City No. 5." After the announcement, the entire venue applauded.

Presentation Ceremony: Immediately following, the presentation ceremony was held. Mayor Yuan Liang read the presentation certificate, bowed, and handed it to Central Government representative Huang Bingheng. The Central Government representative then awarded medals and read out the certificates of commendation, which were accepted by Mayor Yuan Liang. After the ceremony, Huang delivered a speech of thanks.

Various Performances: The ceremony ended at 2:00 PM. The aircraft attached to the string troop performed a flight demonstration, first circling the airfield three times, then entering the city and circling the airspace of Peiping three times before landing simultaneously at Nanyuan Airfield. While the five aircraft were entering the city, Air Force Captain Gao Zhihang piloted one aircraft alone, performing novel maneuvers in the airspace above the airfield, going straight up and down, flipping left and right, hovering briefly like a dragonfly touching water, and then pausing like an eagle watching. His flying skills were superb, and the crowd cheered enthusiastically, especially the students, who were even more enthusiastic, taking off their hats, jumping, and shouting slogans such as "Aviation Saves the Nation" and "China Will Not Perish." Gao performed in the air for half an hour and then landed. The crowd congratulated him. He then went to the stage to shake hands with Mayor Yuan Liang and pay his respects to Central Government representative Huang Bingheng. At 2:45 PM, the five aircraft landed. The five aircraft returned to their unit. After the five aircraft finished their performance, it was already 3:30 PM. The entire group took a photo and dispersed. All sectors have scheduled a propaganda meeting for aviation saving the country at Zhongshan Park at 10:00 AM tomorrow (9th). Central Government representative Huang Bingheng, Captain Gao Zhihang, and others will attend. After the meeting, Gao will lead the five aircraft to leave Peiping and return to their unit, following the Jinpu Railway line south, passing through Tianjin, Jinan, Xuzhou, and other places, landing to refuel as needed. Huang will leave Peiping and return to Beijing within the day to report on his mission. (8th)

(9th)

Songjiang Plans to Dredge the Changshan River

The Xijiao Bridge and Tan area is where rice shops and bran cake industries are located. The huge annual turnover accounts for two-thirds of the county. However, in recent years, due to the Changshan River being silted up, ships from the four villages cannot reach Songjiang directly, which also makes irrigation of farmland difficult. Farmers and merchants in the Songjin counties in the river basin have been asking for dredging for a long time. Now, the county magistrates of Songjin counties have discussed the dredging plan, which requires an estimated cost of 11,000 yuan. Song County will bear 7,000 yuan, and Jin County will raise 4,000 yuan. It is planned to start construction in the middle of the first lunar month. It is reported that this county has raised a sum of 5,000 yuan, which is still 2,000 yuan short. The county government has invited the bran cake industry to raise funds to make this happen.

Department of Civil Affairs Sends Personnel to Inspect General Affairs

The Department of Civil Affairs believes that local general affairs are crucial to the national economy and people's livelihood and should be inspected by personnel to promote them. Luo Ailin was specially sent to this county to investigate accumulated grains, people's livelihood factories, relief homes, public and private charitable organizations, and hospitals. The committee should draft plans for improvement and rectification regarding how to improve general affairs, how to enrich the content, how to economize expenses, how to increase efficiency, how to reorganize the factories already in operation, and how to plan and set up factories that have not yet been set up. The report will be submitted to the committee for verification.

Changshu Rural Farmers Request Power Supply

The electricity plant in this county was previously resolved by the Jiangsu Provincial Electricity Association to allow rural areas to use electricity to irrigate fields. Since October last year, it has been adding rural lines. From east to Hupu and west to Dayiqiao, power has been supplied for lighting. In addition, expansion is still underway. Now, Wu Bofan, the mayor of Meili Town, and others have requested that the Wujiasi Temple and Sijingqiao area in the northern part of Meili, not far from the town, has more than 200 households and more than 5,000 mu of farmland. The commercial market is developed, and there are flower shops and lace factories that need a lot of electricity. Therefore, they have specially requested the district office to forward a letter to the electricity plant to extend the lines to the Wujiasi Temple area to facilitate future agricultural irrigation needs. After the second district chief forwarded the letter to the plant, the plant has sent engineer Huang Zhenxia to the countryside to investigate and consider adding poles for expansion.

Wuxi Winter Feels Like Summer, Broad Beans Bear Fruit

Since last month, the weather in this county has been unusually warm, as if it were the climate of late winter. Vegetables in the rural fields have mostly bloomed. The broad beans planted by Chen Rongchang, a farmer in Gaobang'an Village in the 18th district of the northern township, have all bloomed. Also, the peas in the fields of a farmer named Peng in the township have already borne fruit. In addition, the broad beans planted in the sunny areas of the fields near Dongda'an in the Liutanqiao area of the fifth district have also borne fruit. The early wheat stalks are also mostly stout, no different from the wheat stalks in mid-March. Winter feels like summer, and the plants are abnormal, which has not been seen in previous years.

Two Male Corpses with Gunshot Wounds Found in the Western Suburbs

On the barren mound at Shuigoutou near Yinglong Bridge outside the West Gate, two unnamed male corpses with gunshot wounds were suddenly found yesterday morning (11th). Both male corpses were about twenty years old. The corpses were several feet apart. One corpse was wearing a blue cotton-padded jacket and trousers and yellow basketball shoes. There was a gunshot hole in the right side of the head. The other corpse was wearing a gray cotton-padded jacket and trousers and a black short coat, with a peaked cap on its head. There was a gunshot hole next to the right ear. The corpse was kneeling on the ground, covered in blood, a very tragic sight. Chen Zizhao, the head of the 227th Tu, reported the case to the local branch court, requesting an investigation. At the same time, the Detective Team of the County Public Security Bureau and the Fourth Branch Bureau of the Public Security Bureau in charge of the area dispatched police to investigate. Two ownerless firewood boats were found on the nearby riverbank. On the boats, there was a rattan basket containing galoshes, belts, files, and Gongzhe No. 142 of the Shenxin No. 3 Yarn Factory. These were all seized for investigation and handling.

Inspection of the Total Amount of Old Stamp Duty Registered

The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce has handled the old stamp duty registration for various industries, which was due to end at the end of December of the tenth year. The number and types of public associations, shops, and stamps were separately calculated and listed, with a total amount of 15,745.45 yuan. Yesterday, together with Wu Naiqing, a representative of the Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau, Zhu Fangjian, a representative of the county government, and representatives of various relevant industries, they were jointly inspected. The original sealed packages of old stamp duty were stamped and temporarily sealed and stored in the Chamber of Commerce. After the Ministry of Finance determines the replacement method, it will be processed again. The situation has been reported separately.

Ministry Approves Standards for Business Tax Assessment

The Wine and Soy Sauce Shop Association of Wuxi City believes that the industry has always relied on hot wine as its main business, and has already paid the wine license tax. However, the business tax bureau has repeatedly sent personnel to the stores to investigate and estimate, arbitrarily combining the large amount of wine with the retail sales of small items for assessment, forcing them to pay business tax, resulting in double taxation. In order to avoid disputes and alleviate commercial difficulties, they have specially telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to request an explanation. A reply was received yesterday: "Received the report, checked and found that for shops that mainly engage in tobacco and alcohol and also operate other goods, if the main business part has already paid the tobacco and alcohol license tax, the business tax should be excluded and exempted. The other part that is also operated should still pay business tax to show the difference. If the annual turnover of each store is less than 1,000 yuan, it can be exempted from tax in accordance with the regulations." The association has received the telegram and has passed it on to various stores for compliance.

Robbery and Abduction Case Occurs in the Southeastern Countryside of Danyang

Xu, a villager in Shicun Township in the seventh district of the county, is a small wealthy family and has long been coveted by bandits. At about 10:00 PM the night before, several bandits suddenly rushed into the house, speaking in a northern accent and armed with weapons. They imprisoned Xu's entire family in a room, not allowing them to make a sound. They then looted the house. Before leaving, they abducted a six-year-old boy. Also, the home of a farmer Jing near Huangtang was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits last night, all armed with weapons. They rushed into the house, forbade them to make a sound, ransacked the house everywhere, plundered wealth, and fled without a trace.

Review of the World Economy in 1934 (Continued-2) by Mu Ouchu

The prices of livestock products have also fallen very commonly, with almost no difference between countries. Now, the comparison of the wholesale prices of livestock products in the British market on April 12, 1934, and the same day in 1933 is as follows:

1933 1934

Argentine Beef 3 shillings 6 pence - 4 shillings 3 shillings 4 pence - 3 shillings 8 pence

British Pork 5 shillings - 5 shillings 8 pence 5 shillings 6 pence - 6 shillings 6 pence

Danish Cured Pork 68 shillings - 74 shillings 79 shillings

Danish Butter 90 shillings - 91 shillings 84 shillings

Canadian Cheese 60 shillings - 68 shillings 50 shillings - 58 shillings

(According to the World Economic Yearbook, First Quarter Report, 1934, page 23)

Although the above figures cannot be used as an absolute standard, they can show a glimpse of the agricultural panic. Naturally, the prices of some goods are high. Furthermore, the changes in the prices of major commodities are listed as follows:

New York Cotton New York Raw Silk Chicago Wheat

Per pound Per pound Per Bushel (8 gallons)

Highest Lowest Highest Lowest Highest Lowest

Cents Cents Dollars Dollars Cents Cents

1932 9.20 5.70 1.91 1.10 6.40 43 7/8

1933 11.75 5.90 2.21 1.10 1.60 44 5/8

April to October 1934 12.66 11.76 13.05 12.07 98.3 88.0

(From "Where is the World Going?" Second half of 1934, page 72)

The fall in cocoon prices has been mentioned earlier. As for the rise in cotton prices, it is artificial and should not be seen as a sign of improvement. Both the "Production Reduction Agreement" and "Production Reduction" are facts of artificial price increases.

Since the commodity market is artificially embellished, it naturally affects prices. Therefore, last year, the prices in various countries showed a gradual upward trend, especially in Japan and the United States. The changes in prices in major countries are as follows: (1913 = 100)

Japan England United States Germany France

1932 Highest 139.5 92.2 81.7 100.1 87.0

Lowest 110.6 80.9 71.5 92.0 79.0

1933 Highest 139.8 89.9 98.3 96.1 81.0

Lowest 133.2 82.3 69.0 91.0 78.0

1934 Highest 135.4 92.3 102.8 100.4 79.0

(Up to September) Lowest 131.5 89.5 97.8 95.8 73.0

In nine months, the United States averaged 100.3, a significant increase compared to 83.6 in 1933. However, it is still far from Roosevelt's attempt to return to the 1926 level of 141.4. The highest in the United Kingdom was 92.3, also a significant increase from the previous year and the highest record since 1931. The highest in Japan was 135.4, slightly lower than the highest number in the previous year, but still a relatively high number since 1931. The exception is France, which maintains the gold standard and is lower than the previous year. The highest in Germany was 100.4, also higher than the previous year. However, the decline in France is due to the gold standard. If currency and gold prices are converted, then the decline in France is not as significant as the numbers recorded in the table.

From these price index fluctuations, we can also see the general situation of the world panic over the past year.

With the deepening of the panic, various countries will inevitably face financial crises and financial disturbances. This phenomenon was even more evident in 1934. Because of the urgency of war preparations in various countries, regardless of financial difficulties, they still do not hesitate to pay huge military expenditures. We can see the urgency of the war situation by taking a look at the amount of military spending in various countries.

Japan United Kingdom United States

Military Expenditure Percentage of Expenditure Military Expenditure Percentage of Expenditure Military Expenditure Percentage of Expenditure

1930-31 443 28.4% 111 13. and % 19.7%

1931-1932 454 30.7% 108 14.0% 825 16.5%

1932-33 687 35.2% 103 13.3% 791 15.4%

1933-34 873 38.7% 109 15.7% 716 10.0%

1934-35 938 43.8% 115 16.3% 711 15.8%

(According to "Where is the World Going?" Second half of 1934, page 12. Japanese units are in millions of yen, British in millions of pounds, and American in millions of dollars.)

The increase in military spending in 1934 was a common phenomenon in various countries. The large proportion of expenditures, such as Japan's nearly one-half, is truly astonishing. Although the numerical value of military spending in the United States was slightly less than the previous year, the proportion of expenditures still increased. Because of the increase in military spending and other expenses, the budgets of various countries have a so-called "deficit," so they have to raise public debt as a remedy. The amount of public debt raised by various countries in 1934 was huge and set an unprecedented record, which is also a feature of the world economy in 1934.

The amounts of national debt of major countries in the world for the past seven years are listed as follows:

Japan United Kingdom Germany Italy United States France

Unit Million Yen Million Pounds Million Marks Million Lire Million Dollars Million Francs

1928 5.397 7.631 7.131 88.287 17.604 468.678

1929 5.831 7.620 8.229 88.932 16.931 Unknown

1930 5.959 7.597 9.630 89.877 16.185 482.127 1931 5.0955 7.583 11.342 93.178 16.801 480.770

1932 6.187 7.647 11.434 97.268 19.487 481.188

1933 7.054 7.860 11.690 99.029 22.539 491.899

1934 8.139 8.024 11.793 10.3478 27.053 Unknown

(The fiscal year for Japan, the United Kingdom, Germany, and France ends in March each year, while the fiscal year for Italy and the United States ends in June. According to "Where is the World Going, Second Half of 1934, page 2)

Since the finances of various countries are so strained, the phenomenon of financial turmoil is naturally expected. The scope of financial issues is quite broad, and it is not easy to describe them one by one. Now we will only cite the following two matters for a simple investigation. (To be continued)

The Jian Steamer Ran Aground in Tongzhou Yesterday

Thick Fog, Deeply Sunk in Shallow Waters

The Taikoo Yangtze River steamer Jian, originally sailing in the middle of the Yangtze River, has changed its route to the Yangtze River since the water level has dropped recently. This time, it was loaded with passengers and a large number of goods from Hankou to Shanghai. It was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai yesterday and depart for Hankou today after unloading the goods. However, the ship was not seen entering the port yesterday morning. The company thought that the fog had delayed the journey, and the delay was inevitable, so they didn't pay much attention at first. Little did they know that the ship had arrived near Tongzhou at about 5:00 AM yesterday morning. At that time, it was still dark and the fog on the river was extremely heavy, making navigation very difficult. The ship was obstructed by the fog during the voyage and went off course, mistakenly heading to the sandy beach on the river bank, and the hull became trapped in the shallow water.

Urgent Telegram for Help

When it first ran aground, the captain still wanted to use full power to reverse the ship and drive it back into the river, hoping to escape on its own. However, the ship was fully loaded with passengers and goods, and the draft was very deep. Once it entered the sandy beach, the hull was stuck in the mud and could not move at all. At this point, the captain sent a telegram to Shanghai for help, which the company received at about 4:00 PM.

Dispatching Ships to Lighter Goods

Yesterday afternoon, the company decided that the grounding of the ship could not be solved by towing alone. At a minimum, it was necessary to send a ship to Tongzhou to first unload the passengers and goods from the ship to Shanghai, so that the hull would float on the water and then be towed. After the decision, three large tugboats, C-1, C-3, and Hankou 10, were dispatched, along with a powerful tugboat and more than 100 workers, to work. They rushed to Tongzhou last night to carry out the unloading work. They also sent a telegram to the ship's captain in advance to comfort the passengers on board, saying that the unloading work could begin today.

French Consul General in Shanghai Leaves for Home Today

The Vacant Consul General Position is Succeeded by Mr. Badas

Mr. Badas Has Left France for China to Take Office

Xin Xin News Agency reports that Mr. Mei Liai, the French Consul General in Shanghai, has been transferred back to his country and is scheduled to leave Shanghai today at 3:00 PM with his family on the French postal ship Haili Keluosuo.

The Political Council Will Not Be Abolished

Mr. Wang also said that Mr. Huang Yingbai is scheduled to come to Beijing in the middle of the month to take the position of Minister of the Interior. He does not want to change the position of Chairman of the Political Consolidation Council. There is no discussion of abolishing the council. Mr. Huang's position is like that of Mr. He Jingzhi. Mr. He is the head of the military and political affairs and the head of the Military Branch Council. Now Mr. Huang is the head of internal affairs and the head of the Political Consolidation Council. He can travel between Beijing and Ping anytime to handle everything.

Attitude Towards Hu

Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Mr. Wang also issued a written statement, saying that President Wang arrived in Shanghai this morning, and reporters asked about the various rumors about Mr. Hu Hanmin's actions. Mr. Wang replied that the central government's attitude towards Mr. Hu has not changed in the past three years, namely (1) hoping that Mr. Hu can come to Nanjing to jointly take responsibility, (2) Mr. Hu's criticism in Hong Kong can be accepted, and if there are misunderstandings, they will be explained. If he is driven by emotions and far from the facts, he will not argue, and (3) if Mr. Hu intends to go abroad, the central government will be happy to assist. However, this belongs to Mr. Hu's initiative. The above three points are the central government's attitude towards Mr. Hu for the past three years, which can be proved and has not changed in the slightest.

Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng paid a visit to President Wang at 9:30 AM and talked briefly. Then he accompanied President Wang to the city center area to visit the various constructions of Greater Shanghai. Then he went to the municipal government to visit. During the welcome of all the staff of the municipal government, he gave detailed instructions on all parts of the municipal government. Also, Mr. Wang returned to Beijing by overnight train with Zeng Zhongming at 11:00 PM last night to preside over government affairs.

At that time, Mr. Mei's Chinese and foreign friends and important officials of the French agencies in Shanghai will go to the port to see him off. After Mr. Mei returns to his country, the French Consul General's position in Shanghai will be succeeded by Mr. Badas, who has been appointed by the French government. Mr. Badas has taken the French postal ship Xuenuo Su to China. It is estimated that he will arrive in Shanghai on the 30th of this month to take office. Before Mr. Badas takes office, the position of Consul General will be temporarily held by the French Consul, Mr. Gao Fa. According to the new acting French Consul General, Mr. Badas, he has been in China for more than 30 years and has a good foundation in Chinese. He has served as a Chinese clerk in the French consulates in various parts of China for many years. Then he was promoted to consul and served as consul in Chongqing, Chengdu, Hankou, and other places. Then, last year, when he took office as Consul in Yunnan, he took leave to return to his country. Now he has been promoted to his current position by the government.

The County Baojia System Starts the Third Phase of Work

Since Shanghai County began to implement the Baojia system in November last year, it has been actively carried out, and the work has been very intense. It is now found that the second phase of work has been completed in all districts as scheduled. The township and town heads and Baojia households have been appointed and commissioned. In the trial townships, initially, because the joint guarantee agreement required the Baojia household heads to press their fingerprints, it was quite difficult. After the county government's earnest persuasion and the detailed explanation of the district chiefs and investigators, the township and town heads were able to lead by example and press their fingerprints first. The Baojia household heads also personally pressed their fingerprints. It is heard that in order to urge the completion of the Baojia system as scheduled, County Chief Pan convened a meeting of district chiefs and investigative committee members on New Year's Eve to decide on the third phase of work, which was unanimously started on January 4, and several steps for the progress of the work were agreed upon. The district chiefs, investigators, and district assistants were ordered to go to the townships and Baojia to provide guidance at the same time. In recent days, Wang Xuepeng, the head of the First Section, and the Baojia guidance committee members sent by the Office have also gone to the districts to convene Bao Chief meetings to lecture on the points that should be paid attention to in the third phase of work and the tasks of the Bao Chief to facilitate the progress.

Sea Traffic Was Completely Blocked by Heavy Fog Yesterday

Coastal Merchant Ships Suspended Operations

Yesterday, there was heavy fog in Shanghai, which did not dissipate all day. Many seagoing ships were blocked from entering the port at Wusongkou, and all seagoing ships leaving the port, such as the Ningbo, Chongsha, Wintai, and Chuanshan Haimen routes, were suspended. It can be said that the sea traffic in Shanghai has been blocked by heavy fog.

Anchored at Songkou

Yesterday was the second day of heavy fog in Shanghai. Although the fog outside Wusongkou was not as heavy as the morning of the previous day, it still lingered on the sea surface and could not dissipate all day. The Ningbo route ship still sailed in yesterday. Although the Taikoo Daming, Kuizhou, and Lanyancun's passenger ship Ketiena were able to arrive, they were all delayed. Other seagoing ships, in order to be cautious in navigation, anchored outside Wusongkou, and there were more than ten ships. There were also many ships waiting for the fog to dissipate at Wusong before sailing out.

Seagoing Ships Suspended

Yesterday afternoon, after 4:00 PM, the fog gradually became heavier, and the Pujiang River was hazy and blurred, making it impossible to distinguish objects. It was even more difficult to see anything outside Wusong. The Ningbo route ships Xin Beijing and Xin Ningshao, which sailed to the coastal areas of Zhejiang, decided to temporarily stop sailing due to the heavy fog. They immediately notified the passengers that those who wished to refund their tickets could leave the ship. In addition, the Taizhou Chuanshan Shipu Haimen route ships, as well as the Chongsha route, etc., also temporarily announced the suspension of navigation and did not sail out of the port. Even the North and South Ocean ships were all suspended from sailing out of the port. Sea traffic has been completely blocked by heavy fog.

When the Wind and Waves on the Yangtze River are Huge, the Shanghai-Ping Through Train Stops Crossing the River

On the evening of November 26 last year, when the 301st Shanghai-Ping through train was crossing the river by ferry, it happened to be a time of strong winds and rough waves, and the jolting was quite severe. Afterwards, the Jinpu Railway reported to the Ministry of Railways, requesting that when the wind and waves on the Yangtze River are too large and unfavorable for navigation, all 301st and 302nd crossings should be temporarily suspended from transporting vehicles across the river. Connecting passengers should be transported back and forth by the Chengping ferry. After the passengers and luggage are loaded, all the Shanghai-Ping through trains stopped at the Beijing-Shanghai and Jinpu stations will exchange the up and down train numbers and depart for Shanghai and Ping separately according to the original schedule. After the ministry approved the matter, it was ordered that the Chengping ferry must also determine the wind conditions. If, according to the wind conditions at the time, there is no danger in the Chengping ferry's navigation, the ferry can be used for transportation. Otherwise, it should not be forced to avoid danger.

The Joint Reserve Association of Banks Held the Second Anniversary of the Clearing House

Total Clearing Amount Last Year Was 320 Million

One-Third More Than in 1933

The Clearing House established by the Joint Reserve Association of Shanghai Banks was established on January 10, 1933. It has been handling interbank clearing business with remarkable results. The association held the second anniversary of the Clearing House the night before and held a dinner party to celebrate. The details are as follows:

Dinner Party for Colleagues The association held a dinner party for all Clearing House colleagues in the grand hall of the Xinya Hotel on North Sichuan Road at 7:00 PM the night before. More than 200 clearing members from 38 banks attended the dinner, which was very grand. Zhu Boquan, the manager of the association, was absent due to illness on that day. During the dinner, Deputy Manager Xu Baoqi reported on the work of the past year and the future facilities and improvements on behalf of him. Then Zhang Xingjiu, the representative of the clearing members, delivered a speech of thanks and took a photo to commemorate the event.

Gifts to Add to the Fun The association prepared 10,000 gift certificates from the Joint Gift Company on that day and held a lottery after the dinner to distribute them to the clearing members of each bank to add to the fun.

Last Year's Business Deputy Manager Xu Baoqi reported on the work of the past year, saying that the Clearing House has only been established for two years. The work in the past year has made much progress compared to 1933, which is very gratifying. (2) In the previous year, there were a total of 34 clearing banks, with 64 branches and entrusted banks participating in the clearing. Last year, the number of clearing banks increased by 4 to 38, and the number of branches and entrusted banks increased by 13 to 77. According to the survey, the number of other banking and money industries that entrusted clearing banks to collect bills increased significantly. The scope of clearing has gradually expanded, and the function of clearing has become more and more significant. (2) In the previous year, the total clearing amount for the whole year was 200 million, with more than 900,000 bills. Last year, the total clearing amount for the whole year was 320 million, with more than 1.6 million bills. The clearing amount increased by one-third compared to 1933, and the number of clearing bills increased by two-thirds. The increase in numbers shows the progress of the Clearing House's business. (3) In 1933, the Clearing House's expenses were allocated based on the total amount of bills received and paid by each bank. The expenses were allocated at 1.1 cents per 1,000 yuan of clearing bills, which was 5 to 6 times less than the bill collection fee charged by the industry. Last year, the total clearing expenses for the whole year were calculated at only 8 cents per 1,000 yuan of clearing bills. However, this fee was not allocated by each bank because the Clearing House raised an expense fund last year. Clearing banks have saved a lot of money on industry collection fees since then. (4) The Shanghai Bill Clearing House was established in January two years ago after more than ten years of advocacy. The reason for the delay was entirely due to environmental factors. Although it has only been in operation for two years now, its impact has attracted the close attention of the financial industry in various places. It has progressed from advocacy to implementation. Two months ago, Hangzhou established a joint reserve bank and a bill clearing house. Other places, such as Tianjin and Hankou, will also follow suit soon. This good phenomenon is highly desirable to be universal. In the future, the association's clearing house will continue to plan and work together on improving procedures and habits and promoting business. It will also do its best to advocate and actively promote the establishment of bill clearing houses in the financial industry in various places to seek the welfare of the entire financial industry and make greater contributions to society.

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce Telegraphically Urges the Abolition of Corrupt Taxes and Miscellaneous Levies in Sichuan Province

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce telegraphed the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministries of Finance and Industry, and the Sichuan Provincial Authorities yesterday, saying, "Recently, we received a telegram from the Chengdu Chamber of Commerce in Sichuan Province, saying, 'Since the central government issued a clear order to abolish corrupt taxes and miscellaneous levies, the people of Sichuan, who are suffering from misery, are as happy as if they had seen rain clouds after a long drought. The association telegraphed in support on July 1, hoping that the Sichuan Provincial Authorities would realize the mistakes of the past and think about the difficulties of the future, turn around and change their ways, understand the central government's determination to save the country and preserve its existence, and open a way for the people of Sichuan to escape death and enter life. However, since July of this year, we have only seen other provinces reporting the abolition of corrupt taxes and miscellaneous levies, while there has been no news in Sichuan. Now that the end of the year is approaching, the deadline for complete abolition has arrived. Not only has the order not been followed, but it has become even worse, with more and more levies. According to the complaints of merchants in various industries, the association convened a meeting of members and submitted the matter for discussion. After public decision, the Sichuan Provincial Authorities have not followed the central government's laws and regulations to abolish corrupt taxes and miscellaneous levies. Our merchants in various industries should not regard the central government's laws and regulations as a mere formality. They should only follow the order to automatically abolish them when the deadline expires at the end of December. At that time, we hope that the central government and the provincial party and government will severely punish those who violate the order to collect corrupt taxes and miscellaneous levies, and provide practical protection to those who follow the order to automatically abolish corrupt taxes and miscellaneous levies, so as to preserve their credibility and show compassion to the remaining people.' The matter has been recorded in the minutes. The association has the responsibility to implement it and does not dare to keep it from the higher authorities. We hereby telegraph to your government, the Executive Yuan, and the ministries for review and approval. We earnestly request that you grant our request and order the immediate abolition of corrupt taxes and miscellaneous levies to relieve the people's suffering. Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China, kowtows."

Ji Sheng Hui's Investigation Report on the Severe Disaster in Haiyan

The China Ji Sheng Hui (Relief Society) appointed Li Jun Yunmen as the Director of Haiyan Relief, who, along with relief volunteers, went to investigate. According to reports, Changlong, after meeting with Magistrate Jin and various agencies, immediately requested and reviewed Magistrate Jin's map of Haiyan County. The next day, he rushed to the designated Zones 4, 5, and 6 (Zone 4 was originally designated as half a zone, but because the area was too small to divide, the entire zone was included) for detailed inspection. Zone 5 was found to be the most severely affected, followed by Zones 4 and 6, with little difference between the latter two. However, in the western part of Zone 4, a small number of people rely on seawall construction and salt production for their livelihood. The strong can barely survive, while the weak can hardly find food. Zone 6 has a large area and a large population, with many people making a living as peddlers. In this time of famine, not to mention small businesses, even merchants are struggling to survive. Therefore, the disaster situation in Zones 4, 5, and 6 is roughly the same. In Haiyan's rural areas, silk cocoons are the main product, followed by rice and wheat. Last year's drought was unprecedented in nearly a century. Not only was there no harvest of rice and grain, but the silkworm industry also suffered severely. Last summer, there was no rainfall, and rivers dried up. All ponds, which were normally relied upon for irrigation, were dry and exposed at the bottom. Farmers had no way to draw water, and after exhausting all means, the rice seedlings that had already sprouted became weeds, and the autumn rice turned into empty shells. Rural areas went bankrupt, and the disaster was even more severe than in Haining. Changlong witnessed the gaunt faces of the disaster victims. The homes of the people were all but empty. Some disaster victims were living on gruel, while others were filling their stomachs with wild vegetables and chaff. There were also many people leading the old and carrying the young to beg in other counties, one after another. Many people died of hunger and disease, and their corpses were left unburied for days because their families could not afford to buy coffins. Along the way, there were reports of people selling their wives and snatching rice to survive, a scene of utter desolation, too tragic to bear. As a result, bandits have risen up and robbery is rampant. The weak are left in ditches, and the strong take risks. This is indeed the reality, too painful to witness, leaving only tears to shed. Now that it is deep winter, hunger and cold are intertwined, and people are desperately waiting for help. The relief funds and clothing here are not enough to meet the huge need, making it difficult to distribute. This is a detailed report of the situation, and it is hoped that additional grace will be bestowed. The reported misery is too difficult to read. Without food or clothing, how can they survive the year? The members of the society are ashamed of their lack of ability to provide relief, and only hope that comrades in the country will rise up to save this remnant of the population by economizing on food and clothing.
