Yao Xiao'an Wang Pingqiu Qilin Leopard

Zhongxi (1040) 11:00 AM to 12:00 PM

Opening Chapter "Baochai Catches a Butterfly"

Light clouds and drizzle brew a spring shade. Casting aside idle worries, ascend Cui Ting. The blooming flowers and chirping birds cease. Suddenly, a pair of butterflies chase fragrant dust. Fluttering, they resemble a brocade of flowers. Rising and falling, they are like birds entering the forest. It must be an accident that they resemble swallows. When playing in the water, they want to imitate dragonflies. Baochai carries a silk fan and gently taps. One sees her jade sleeves slightly wet and her fragrant sweat dripping. Passing through the winding gallery, pushing aside flowers and willows with care. Just as she was about to catch them, she lamented that she could not. Suddenly, she heard whispered words through the water. Baochai was alert and able to transform. She walked past the Qingfang Bridge but hesitated. She loudly called Pin'er on purpose. She shifted the blame to Jiangdong, killing Bo. Xiaohong was very jealous when she heard this. From then on, she planted the seeds of disaster in Xiaoxiang. What a waste of effort.

Li Huichiu White Snake Legend

Yuanchang (1120) 11:30 AM to 12:30 PM

Opening Chapter "The Five Senses Fight"

Mouth, nose, eyebrows, ears, eyes. Having five senses upright makes a person. The mouth says that I can speak all the languages of the world. Speaking of heaven and earth, nothing is not precise. Laughing nose. Falsely claiming honor. Actually sitting high in the middle. Nose brother listen. Hmph one sound. I advise you to keep your mouth as tight as a bottle. I am able to smell and am very intelligent. Embracing the nose and chanting poetry has a phoenix-like elegance. To matters, the eyes have me on top. The white eyes often look at the people of the world. The inborn tendency to be snobbish is the most ruthless. The eyes listen and the pupils open. Saying I can distinguish five colors and distinguish gold and silver. Xiang Yu had double pupils and prospered the country. Guan Gong's phoenix eyes have prestige. Only the eyebrows claim to be discarded. Asking what virtue and ability he has. Surprisingly sitting on the highest level. The eyebrows wrinkle and will answer. Saying that there are no eyebrows on the face of the Atiao people. Moreover, drawing eyebrows is a pleasure for the Jingzhao boudoir. Xi Shi frowned and bathed in the Emperor's grace. Not as ugly as the ears. Strange shapes like chaos. How can you sell close to your face? The old ears listen and scratch their ears. Saying that I am good at listening to music and telling stories in every way. Pretending to be foolish and deaf is my forte. Able to listen to the walls and be good at preventing people. The five senses were arguing. Fortunately, the tip of the tongue came out to persuade the villagers. Saying that our gates are connected to each other and we are born as one. Why bother making a mess today? If people know about it, how can they maintain their faces?

National Studies

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Continuing the Farewell Poem from Dreaming of Mount Tianmu — Li Bai

The clouds are green, about to rain, the water ripples, producing mist.

Lightning flashes, thunder rumbles, hills and mountains collapse, the stone door of the cave suddenly opens.

The vastness of the green sky is bottomless, the sun and moon shine on golden and silver platforms.

Rainbows are clothes and wind is the horse, the lords of the clouds come down in droves.

Tigers beat the zither, phoenixes circle the chariot, the immortals are arranged like hemp.

Suddenly my soul shivers and my spirit trembles, I wake up in shock and let out a long sigh.

I only feel the pillows and mats of the time, losing the mist and haze of the past.

The joys of the world are also like this; all things in ancient times flow eastward like water!

When will I return after leaving you? I will let the white deer roam among the green cliffs.

I will ride and visit famous mountains when I want to go. How can I bow my eyebrows and bend my waist to serve the powerful

Making me unable to be happy?

Page 25

Shen Bao Local Supplement Movie Special

The Essence and Production of Newsreels (Part 1)

— Huang Yingdai

A Historical Record

Value Determined by the Significance of Events

When we go to the cinema, besides the main feature, there are also cartoons and newsreels. This article will discuss the essence and production of newsreels. In short, the value of a newsreel is determined by the magnitude of the event it captures. An ordinary newsreel cannot be screened again after a considerable period. However, if the event is significant or has major political implications, it may be shown again even after several years, decades, or even centuries. This is because newsreels, in essence, represent a page of historical record, and their value is further enhanced by the fact that history books only use text to record events, while newsreels can project the real events on the screen, perhaps making them even more valuable than historical records.

As for the production of newsreels, speed and distinctiveness are paramount. After an event occurs in Europe or America, it can be seen on screen in Shanghai in less than one or two months. The brevity of this time and the speed of production cannot but amaze us. Moreover, the danger faced by the crew and their courageous spirit during filming sometimes leave us speechless! Some newsreels may be quite ordinary, but if a military parade is scheduled, and the king is to personally inspect it, but on that day, a change occurs and the king does not attend the parade, and it is inspected by other officials, wouldn't the value of the newsreel be diminished by the king's absence? Conversely, if the king were to be injured in a car accident en route to the parade, or assassinated, resulting in a tragedy, the newsreel crew would have an unexpected gain. The event is magnified, and the value of the newsreel itself is increased. However, at the beginning of filming, the film company would never have dreamed that such a tragedy could occur and such a valuable newsreel could be captured.

Not long ago, Shanghai screened the Fox Film Corporation's "Marseilles Tragedy" newsreel. To help readers understand the production process of newsreels, it is worth describing the beginning and end of the "Marseilles Tragedy" filming. The Marseilles Tragedy occurred on October 9th, and by the end of November, the newsreel of the Marseilles Tragedy was being screened in Shanghai. The interval was only forty or fifty days, and it was also hindered in the middle; otherwise, it could have been earlier. This visit to France by King Alexander of Yugoslavia was indeed an important page in political history. Therefore, on the day of his arrival in France, cameramen from various film companies gathered in Marseilles, preparing to film various news events. The estimated value of this newsreel was initially ordinary. However, the assassination of Alexander and the death of Barthou in the same car suddenly increased the value of the newsreel, which was an unexpected gain. Before Fox Film Corporation produced the "Marseilles Tragedy" newsreel, they dispatched four cameramen: the Mackie brothers, George, and Lemoine. They were all members of Fox's French filming team. The work was divided as follows: Lemoine filmed the scene of the King of Yugoslavia landing at the dock, George recorded the sound of the empty car carrying the King driving through the streets of Marseilles, and the Mackie brothers filmed fragmented shots.

After the car carrying King Alexander and French Foreign Minister Barthou drove off, George stopped recording sound and switched to a handheld camera, following the King's car closely. Lemoine switched to recording sound, followed the honor guard, and also kept an eye on the street for news that could be filmed. When Alexander's car reached the stock exchange area, a tall man suddenly jumped onto the running board from the crowd, shouting "Your Majesty!" The guards hesitated, wondering if this man was an assassin or a drunken royalist? But in less than a second, an unexpected tragedy had occurred. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "Repainting the Eyebrows"

— You Jing

Let's Try Again——Grand Shanghai

It is a painful thing in the human world when husband and wife have emotional rifts but have to maintain a superficial harmony, living together but dreaming different dreams. If the author understands and grasps it properly when making it into a work of art, it can become a valuable and successful work.

"Repainting the Eyebrows" is a film about a couple without love. The main reason it did not succeed is not that it "portrays love disputes or boredom," but that the author did not understand the essence of such problems.

Dr. Jia Ke and his wife, Alice, lost their love after ten years of marriage. The man fell in love with a dancer due to professional opportunities. The woman fell in love with her unmarried nephew-in-law, Paul.

Later, Paul broke off with Alice, the married woman, for the sake of his fiancée's happiness, who was already pregnant. Jia Ke also abandoned the dancer halfway due to a so-called discovery of conscience to rekindle the ashes of love, and Alice actually allowed him to repaint her broken sad eyebrows.

Here, the author painstakingly made a reformist sermon, but how can it be as ruthless as the facts!

The performance is also not very good. The whole film is loose, not lively, and not tense. Adapted from a stage play - the original author is Vincent Lawrence - but it fails to adopt the compact and concise advantages of stage plays for application in film art, only inheriting the shortcomings of the stage play's monotonous background, lengthy dialogue, and one-line development, such as the pregnancy of the niece, Maggie, and the union of Paul and Maggie, etc., without concise and essential scenes to set off. Even the main key to the reunion of Jia Ke and Alice lacks the necessary and sufficient process, relying entirely on dialogue to advance the plot, which is not a good technique of film art.

Naturally, there are also some commendable aspects, such as the music, which plays a very good role here. When Alice returns from a night party and receives cold treatment from her husband, and strolls in the moonlight, the melancholy and desolate music silently conveys the inner feelings of this boudoir woman. When Paul kisses her, a tune that seems to be happy in sadness is played, but it quickly turns into a melancholy tone as her skirt is torn. This exchange of music and moonlight poetically expresses the mood and changes experienced by the characters in the play. However, when the author uses the dance music of the club to stimulate the heroine at the end, as the key to her change of heart, it is too abrupt and comical after she just said, "Champagne is good, but unfortunately youth is no longer, and love is tired and old."

Other examples include the use of Paul tearing Alice's skirt to symbolize the breakdown of their love. When Alice eats dinner alone, the long candle shadows and candle tears are used to express her sorrow in the dream and disillusionment of love. And the small things like inserting flowers in a vase also show the discord between husband and wife, all of which are lovely little cleverness.

Weaving the dancing and healing section of the dancer before the game is simply clumsy and superfluous, which can be cleverly inserted in the middle.

In terms of actors, Diana Wynyard and Clive Brook are not as successful as in "Random World and Autumn", but the former is better. Arthur Hoyt, who plays the male servant Philip, performs quite well.

Film & Comics Telephone

— Luo Ping

Someone asked: "Why do critics have to force an artist to draw materials from the reality around him, instead of letting him create his kingdom in his rich ideals?"

Then comes an arbitrary conclusion that only a few people who, like them, do not fully understand the essence of art will believe, "The greatness of an artist does not lie in his ability to faithfully imitate reality."

Yes, the greatness of an artist does not lie in his ability to faithfully "imitate" (?) reality, but in his ability to correctly analyze reality, understand reality, and see through reality!

Anyone with a little cultivation will not deny that art is a reflection of objective existence, and no one will deny the possibility of explaining art with life. Only works that are closer to life and more authentic can move people's hearts more.

Some say that the greatness of an artist lies in his ability to use his genius and learning to create a realm of reality, so that the common people, no, so that a few gentlemen can gain a moment of liberation in their narrow reality.

However, may I ask, can a work of art be created by relying solely on an artist's genius and learning? At least, he has to express something, and these things are the reflection of objective existence through the author's concepts.

Even the bull-headed horse-faced, Frankenstein, the fat doctor's jade legs, and everything that gentlemen love are by no means things that an artist can imagine out of thin air using only his genius and learning, but are all reflections of objective existence through the writer's concepts.

Audience Opinion

Words on "Rebirth Flower"

— Er Yin

"Sister Flowers" once captured the general public, and "Rebirth Flower" still captures the general public.

The content unfolds as expected, and everything is suitable for most viewers, such as the elderly and women...

The director's surgery is naturally very brilliant. As for the control of the structure, I think the passage in which Wang Xianzhai gets money from Fang Dabao and the others is very appropriate, taking advantage of people's unexpectedness to make the audience stunned until the confession under the stairs.

The actors, Hu Die and Xuan Jinglin, show no signs of disappointment at all. Wang Xianzhai and Tan Zhiyuan are excellent. The latter especially exerts his talents as much as possible, and Mei Xi and Zhao Yue are also competent.

One thing that makes people feel a little short of perfection: Zheng Xiaoqiu, who plays Tao Ge, is too that. He simply doesn't know how to perform more profoundly. In the whole play, only the scene of getting drunk is more competent.

"Catching people, catching people" exposes the oppression of the revolutionary army by the warlords in the past, making people feel that the progressive youth at that time were really extremely painful. I was especially moved by this point.

"Rebirth Flower" this tail, after all, did not backfire, this is what I am offering to the Mingxing Company to celebrate.

Movie Novel

Forsaking All Others (Part 1)

— Su Yin

Produced by MGM of the United States, starring Joan Crawford, Clark Gable, etc.

By this time tomorrow, she will be Mrs. Dylan Duda. This seems unbelievable, but it is true. At this time, Mary Clay was lying comfortably on the massage bed in her magnificent bedroom, letting the masseuse named Bella beat and support her. While lying down, she counted the past. She had loved Dylan since she was seven or eight years old. She, Dylan, and another, Jeffrey Williams, grew up together. They were close friends, childhood sweethearts, and like brothers and sisters. Speaking of Dylan's character, he was naturally unrestrained and had never had any sorrows. No matter what happened, he would always laugh and not take it seriously. At that time, Mary was a little girl with long legs, big eyes, and fluffy hair. Her liking for Dylan was because of his natural generosity. Jeffrey's nature was much more serious. From a young age, he showed a thoughtful attitude. He was always by Mary's side. When she fell and hurt her kneecap, he was always there to comfort her. When there was a fight, he always protected her. Sometimes, when Dylan unintentionally offended her, Jeffrey was always there to comfort her.

Later, everyone grew up. Jeffrey also went out to Spain. He said he was going to make a fortune, he said with a smile. Dylan, on the other hand, was still happily happy, carefree, plus elegant, talented, and easy to win the hearts of women... Not bad, he had a lingering woman in Paris, but now it has been left behind. In less than twenty-four hours, he will marry Mary Clay. In Mary's mind, there is only this thing that makes her feel thrilling. She is now covered with a thick layer of ointment on her face, and her fluffy hair is tied to the side with a ribbon, but in less than twenty-four hours, she will be a bride. At this time, Bella also did not know what to think, occasionally lost in thought, and patted Mary heavily on the back. Mary was taken aback and shouted, "Hey, Bella, be careful... I don't want to see in tomorrow's newspaper: The newly married is so beautiful, her back is blue and purple, mottled and grotesque..." Bella angrily threw Mary's braids aside, and then said, "Blue or purple, black or yellow, it's too boring to get married." She said, supporting hard, Mary did not say a word, let her arrange.

After a while, the door opened, Mary leaned over, half climbed up, Paula jumped in. Paula is petite and exquisite, dressed like a foreign doll, always jumping when walking. Mary almost brought her up since she was a child. When she saw Mary lying on the bed, Bella was beating her, she couldn't help opening her mouth and shouting, "Mary! Your wedding is about to begin, why are you still lying there and letting someone beat you? Bella, don't beat her! Everyone in the house is waiting for you to go down! Why are you lying there as if nothing happened... I bought things all afternoon, everything is done, my waist is going to be paralyzed. What? You think I haven't seen a wedding before?" Mary said with a smile, "Baby Paula, I can't do without you, I simply can't do it. You must know these things..." Bella pretended to sigh, "How can she not know? Didn't she already bury three men?" Bella has been working under Paula for a long time, so it doesn't matter if she is more presumptuous. Paula was not angry at all, she also said, "You're wrong. I only buried two husbands. I don't know where the third one went." Bella said, "Probably he went to foreign exile." Paula ignored her and just looked at Mary and asked her happily, "Happy?" Mary said, "No, I feel like I'm going to die or faint before I walk in front of the altar." Paula reminisced about her own experience and comforted her, "It doesn't matter. The first time is always like this." But someone was knocking on the door outside, interrupting Paula's words. (To be continued)
